THE CUSTOM ORDINANCE
Order under Section 19A
BY Virtue of the power vested in me under Section 19 (A) of the Customs Ordinance (Chapter 235), as amended by the 
Customs (Amendment) Law No. 35 of 1974 and the Customs (Amendment) Act, No. 83 of 1988, I, Basil Rajapaksa, 
Minister of Finance do by this Order exempt the goods speciﬁ  ed in Column V of the Schedule hereto, imported by or 
consigned to person or institutions speciﬁ ed in the corresponding entry in Column II of that Schedule from payment of the 
Customs Import Duty, Leviable thereon as speciﬁ  ed in the corresponding entry in Column VIII of that Schedule subject to 
such conditions.
 However, any importer or person by whom or on whose behalf any goods, speciﬁ  ed and imported under this Order 
are subsequently to be sold or disposed of contrary to the conditions speciﬁ  ed, such importer or person shall obtain prior 
approval of the Director General of Customs and pay the Customs Import Duty payable on such goods at the time of sale or 
disposal to the Director General of Customs in terms of Section 19 (A) (3). Any goods sold or disposed of in contravention 
of such Section shall be liable to be forfeited.
Bൺඌංඅ Rൺඃൺඉൺ඄ඌൺ,
Minister of  Finance.
Ministry of Finance,
Colombo 01,
November 29, 2021.
